Collection of Words by Rev. Sun Myung Moon Volume 16  
Compiled by the Committee for the Compilation of Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words  

Foreword                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1) Restoration through Indemnity and Selection of Holy Grounds  
<Summary of Words> Humans can offer a lesser value of indemnity conditions to God, but cannot do so to Satan. Equal value indemnity conditions must be established for Satan. Lesser value indemnity conditions can exist between humans and God, but such lesser value conditions do not hold between humans and Satan. Therefore, to establish indemnity conditions for Satan, one must give what God loves the most. Thus, when establishing indemnity conditions, it must be done with love equal to that of the original being. If God wants to establish A as an indemnity condition, that A must be something that God Himself loves. This introduces the issue of heart. Therefore, the Messiah must be someone who can be loved equally by the created world. God sent Jesus to restore the world. The indemnity conditions of the Unification Church are established by the teacher, and you must follow. You cannot unify the earthly world without unifying the spiritual world. You cannot unify earthly humans without unifying the angels. Therefore, first unify the spiritual world and have the spiritual world cooperate with the earthly world. December 21, 1965 (Tuesday) at 10:30 AM, Suwon. * This statement was made in Suwon during the national pilgrimage of holy grounds and was organized from notes taken by former president Yoo Ho-won. The title was added by the editor.  

8   Restoration through Indemnity and Selection of Holy Grounds  
The teacher came out with a mission along with liberation. At that time, Dr. Lee had a desire. If Christianity had joined hands with me then, we could have reached a global standard within seven years, that is, before the teacher turned 33. It should have been so. We had to overcome one peak both internally and externally, but the teacher crossed it alone. That is why he entered the northern region, the valley of suffering. The seven-year course of resurrection was walked by the teacher alone, and the seven-year course of growth was walked by the members as well. We must meet with the leaders of the nation at the last peak and cross the national seven-year peak, and then we must cross the global peak. Korea is an Abel-type nation, so it must indemnify vertically. Such indemnity conditions must also be established in Cain-type nations. After finding people, we must find the land. The reason the teacher toured 40 countries was for the selection of holy grounds. Because the standard before the fall was established in Korea, holy grounds could be selected. 105 holy grounds were selected in 40 countries worldwide. The 120 families symbolize 120 nations. In the future, we must select 120 holy grounds. In Korea, we must find 72 locations centered around the number 70 and establish conditions. There must be more holy grounds than in the United States. The selection of holy grounds means being in a position similar to that of creating the land before creating humans. When the saints stand here, it is as if humans and the land have been created. That is why the angelic world and the spiritual world must cooperate. Therefore, having 120 holy grounds means having the territory of 120 nations. In selecting holy grounds in the United States, their ancestors will be mobilized to cooperate. The period for selecting holy grounds starts from December 31, 1964, and January 1, 1965, and lasts until December 31, 1965, and January 1 to 4, 1966. It must span three years in terms of lunar years. The number 6 is the number that Satan has invaded. Therefore, this number must be restored through indemnity. The resolution of the Korea-Japan issue also stems from this number 6. The Korea-Japan issue will be resolved 60 years after the Eulsa Treaty. Because Jesus came to the earth and was abandoned by his parents, the teacher cannot evangelize his parents. *  

2) The Reason for Evangelism  
<Summary of Words> Even if we cannot eliminate the desires of the body, if we strengthen the power of the mind that controls the body, we can govern the body. So how can we strengthen this mind? The human mind moves below the level of the fallen nature. Once we cross this line, the mind can go directly to God. Then, a purpose arises, and a direction is established. This also creates circumstances and feelings. Purpose, direction, and circumstances correspond to ideology, action, and life. Good seeks to stand in the position of the object before God, while evil seeks to stand in the position of the subject. Jesus came as the perfect object. According to the principle of creation, the relative ideology that could not be realized on earth cannot be realized in the spiritual world either. However, if we establish children of faith on earth and stand in the position of parents who are not our biological parents, we can finally realize this ideology. This is the reason we must evangelize. *  
December 22, 1965 (Wednesday) at 10 AM, Anyang. * This statement was made in Anyang during the national pilgrimage of holy grounds and was organized from notes taken by former president Yoo Ho-won. The title was added by the editor.  

3) What is a Family Member?  
Matthew 26:36-46  
<Prayer (I)> Father! Yesterday, all the people praised your will and celebrated the day your son was born. However, how many children can truly say they have served you and fulfilled their duty before you? How many children would you like to present with pride? When we think of this, we cannot help but worry that your sorrow will deepen. Now, having passed that one day, we face a new day of prostration and worship before you, so let this lonely day become a holy day before your will. We sincerely hope and wish that you grant us strength and ability to create a new history. We know well that without your heart of compassion and love, we could not prostrate ourselves before you in this manner today. We are embarrassed that we have not prepared ourselves adequately before you, but we earnestly ask for your acceptance. On this December 26, 1965 (Sunday), we offer our scattered hearts to serve you faithfully. * The prayer part of this statement was organized from a tape, and the word part was organized from <Seonghwa> No. 53 (March 1, 1966), No. 54 (April 1, 1966), No. 55 (May 1, 1966), No. 58 (August 1966), and No. 59 (September 1966).  

12   What is a Family Member?  
It is time to reflect. When we think about where our hearts are directed and how our bodies have prostrated before you, we feel only a sense of inadequacy. With such hearts, we pray for your acceptance, so please embrace us and have compassion on us. Many people in this nation long for your will to be fulfilled and await the day you will come, but there are countless people who do not know that day or that will. We earnestly hope and wish that you grant them heavenly grace so that they may know the path they should take, and that their bodies and hearts may align with the direction you desire. Father! Please have compassion on the lonely brothers of unification scattered across South Korea. Do not let us forget that the time to pledge the final battle is approaching, and let us serve you with all our loyalty and intellect. Regardless of the effort and sacrifice, we earnestly hope and wish that we can make a new determination and resolution to fulfill this will left to us. We entrust all things to you at this time, so please govern from beginning to end, and we pray all these words in your name. Amen.  
<Prayer (II)> As we trace back through the long history filled with sorrowful days, who knows your heart that had to tread through such paths? Who understands your circumstances, and who knows your hopes? You alone know that heart, that situation, and that feeling and will. Please allow us to feel once again how pitiful you are for having worked to find a child who can teach humanity about your hopes, circumstances, and feelings, which they do not understand. That person is not someone else but our Father, who must live with us forever, and he is not someone who must toil but the Lord who created the universe. Please let us know that he is our Father and our true Lord, who must embrace and love the entire universe. We must become children who can feel the sorrow of the historical twists and turns he has endured. When we think that the mistake of our ancestors has become an unforgivable sin over countless ages, let them realize that no matter how much tears and blood they shed, they cannot repay it, and even sacrificing their lives a million times cannot repay it. Today, as we gather on the last Sunday of 1965, please have compassion on us. You who have walked the difficult paths of history, please see our failure to let this year pass with sorrow. You wished to present this group of unification to the 30 million people of the nation, so that they could glorify you together with the people, but we have failed to fulfill our responsibilities and are sending this year away with tears. Please allow us to send this year away with tears. May 1966 be welcomed with a new determination and new faith, and let this time be one of repentance for the conditions of lamentation we left before you, and a time to vow for a new start. Who among us can say they know you? Who among us can say they will establish your will? Who among us can pledge to give their life for you? When we realize that there is no one, let us, who have gathered here, though pitiful and insignificant, be those who once pledged loyalty to you and vowed to give our lives for you. If there are weary ones among us, please give them strength, and if there are discouraged ones, please hold them. We have been trampled by the mockery of our enemies and carry unspeakable sorrows from our sad past history. Let us not become those who lose sight of all those painful feelings. Please do not let us forget your sorrow and your resentment. When you judge this sinful world, may we be your children who can appear as victors who can surely glorify you. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.  

14   What is a Family Member?  
On this day, countless children have prostrated before your knees. If there are children who make promises and pray before you as the new year approaches, please bestow special grace upon them. Let them settle all their past inadequacies and prepare themselves to stand before you in the new year, knowing how to adorn and equip themselves. At home, they must be equipped as filial children, and when they go out, they must be armed to fight against enemies. We earnestly hope and wish that you protect our path and guide us. At this time, as insignificant people gather, please bind our hearts together as one. Let us critically reflect on who our hearts have come out for and what direction our bodies have taken, so that we can offer everything before you at this time. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. In the past, we have lived with hearts of joy and sorrow, but in the new year, let us be those who can start with new determination. At this time, our inadequate forms have prostrated before you, so please stretch out your hand of compassion and embrace us, and grant us new commands. We earnestly ask this, praying all these words in your name. Amen.  
<Prayer (III)> We know that Jesus came to this earth and walked a path filled with many twists and turns for over 30 years. We cannot help but feel heartbroken when we think that we have not been able to welcome you on any one day and have not been able to fulfill our loyalty before you. Yesterday, all the people celebrated the day Jesus was born. However, how much have you longed for the true image of Jesus Christ being welcomed? At this time, let us know how to yearn for the true image of Christ and the true sons and daughters of the Father that heaven and earth desire. Thus, let this time be clean and beautiful, allowing us to correct our inadequate postures. We earnestly hope and wish for this.
15 There are many who revere heaven, but few who are willing to take responsibility for heaven. We must take responsibility for heaven. We know that the path to heaven is good, but we also recognize that many people try to avoid the thorny path that lies along that road. Father! You have worked tirelessly for us for countless ages. Yet today, humanity seeks to avoid the arduous path necessary to walk the way of heaven, the true path, and wishes to entrust our sorrow and pain to you, so we earnestly hope for your forgiveness. Today, the group of unification is gathered before you. Unlike others, we understand your heart, but unlike your circumstances, we have acted according to our own will regarding the path of hope you left behind, and we have refused to dedicate our lives. We ask that you allow us to honestly reveal ourselves before you in this hour. We pray to walk the path of life according to your will. We must walk the path of death with you, the thorny path with you, and the path of being forsaken with you. Your will is good, and the path you have set is a good path, yet we are not good. Please accept our unworthy selves and forgive our past shortcomings. We have the desire to live with you, so Father, we earnestly hope that you will look upon us with compassion and embrace us. No matter what anyone says, I cannot deny that I am your son or daughter, and I earnestly hope to be established as a child who can struggle with that truth. We have the justification of being your children, bound by love and a blood relationship that cannot be severed from you, so we know that nothing can deny our relationship with you. May we repent for not having been true sons and daughters and humbly approach you to seek forgiveness. Even if our Father appears ugly and shabby, he is undoubtedly our Father, and even if he bears a sorrowful heart and worries, he is undoubtedly our Father. We must understand what it means to be a family and know that we have not been filial to you. We earnestly hope to become your children who can recognize this. Who do you want to meet? With whom do you wish to make a promise? To whom do you want to share your many grievances? We hope that you will do so for us today. If you are indignant and resentful, we too are indignant and resentful. Therefore, we earnestly hope that you will make us your children who can be strong and courageous enough to fight against the enemy. Who can inform you of your circumstances, and who can teach you about your heart? Only you can do that. We know that when we appear before you with a heart that desires your compassion, even in our inadequate and shabby state, you cannot forsake us. Please have compassion on us as we call you Father with a heart full of sorrow. We earnestly hope for a new day that can take responsibility for a new historical relationship, and we wish to welcome the new year. We earnestly ask that you make us your sons and daughters who can bear the grief of not being able to fulfill our filial duty and loyalty on the foundation of your heart until the day of ultimate victory. At this time, Father, as we stand at the altar, may the heart of the one delivering the message and the heart of those receiving it not be divided. Open the door of our hearts with your heart, move our circumstances, and observe our current reality, removing all conditions that cannot bring you joy. Please leave only the conditions that can bring you joy, come to us, become our heart's friend, and dwell in our lives so that we can become sons and daughters who can fulfill the mission of pioneers. If there are any elements that hinder us from serving you, please remove them, and allow this time to be one where only you can be served and only you can command. We pray all these things in your name. Amen. 

<Words> When you first enter the Unification Church, you may find it strange that the members use the term "family" unlike ordinary church members. However, the term family is a noun used among those who are in the closest relationships in the world. Therefore, you must clearly understand the significance of the term family and use it accordingly. God, who judges the world of evil and seeks to establish the world of good, you must know that this world we currently live in is not a good world. Anyone you ask will tell you that this world is an evil world. Then, despite the countless people who have come forth hoping for good, how has this world become an evil world instead of a good one? This has become the greatest anguish for those who harbor a purpose. We know well that sacrifices must be made to solve this problem. Many have pursued goodness with a sincere heart, but no one has longed for evil with a sincere heart. However, when we see that the evil that people do not pursue or long for is greater than good, we can infer that today’s world did not start from good but from evil. Therefore, if God exists, He must provide a way for humanity to go towards good. Evil individuals have given rise to evil families, and those families have come together to form evil societies, evil nations, and today the entire world is under the dominion of evil. We understand well that this was not the original wish of humanity nor the wish of God. Therefore, if God exists, He must inevitably carry out a new providence that can eliminate the evil of this world and settle the evil of this world. Since we cannot leave the evil world as it is, a movement must be initiated to establish the world that God desires. This movement must start from one family and spread to society, nations, and the world. We know well that the concept of the chosen people of Israel emerged on the historical path. So, who established that? We must understand that it was God who established it through historical connections to expand the foundation of new goodness. In this way, individuals were established to wage war against evil individuals, families were established to set standards of victory against evil families, and tribes, nations, and states were established to eliminate the evil world and establish good tribes, good nations, and good states. We cannot deny that God prepared a time and a nation to send one who could bear the overall responsibility to establish the will of the whole world on behalf of the world. Who is that person? That person must be one who can save evil people centered on goodness in an evil world, and that person is none other than Jesus Christ. 

The Mission of Jesus Christ So what mission did he come to this earth with? His mission was to restore the evil world and establish a good world, so he must come to this earth in the position of the only begotten son who can receive the deepest love of God, that is, in the position to represent the heart of God's love and call God Father. Therefore, Jesus Christ is the only begotten son of God. History testifies that Jesus came to this earth as the king of good kings to establish God's will. Thus, the people of Israel were to unite centered on Jesus. Today, in this evil world, humans live their social lives centered on themselves. Their views on society, the nation, the world, and the universe are all things that can only align with evil within the realm of corruption. Still, on this earth, there has not yet appeared a personal life, social life, national life, global life, or cosmic life that can connect with God and align with goodness. Therefore, what Jesus Christ wanted to convey during his life on this earth was the overall will of God. Jesus came with the mission to conclude all hopes of history, to fight against the evil of the age, to eradicate evil, and to usher in a day of victory centered on a good nation to establish himself as the King of Kings. This was the fundamental responsibility and purpose for which Jesus came to this earth. Therefore, to establish this foundation, Jesus had to lay the groundwork for personal victory, family victory, tribal victory, national victory, and the victory of the world on this earth. He had to establish his worldview and lifestyle on that foundation. Since God could not foresee how Jesus' life would unfold, He hoped for a day when Jesus could win in personal battles, family battles, tribal battles, national battles, and ultimately, a day of victory. We must understand that God raised the chosen people with this hope in mind. 

The People of Israel Who Could Not Receive Jesus So what should have been the hope of this chosen people? They should have replaced their worldview, life view, and cosmic view with the worldview, life view, and cosmic view of Jesus Christ, who came as the King of Kings to this earth. However, at that time, the people of Israel could not receive Jesus in that position. As a result, they could not bring forth the results of goodness that could conclude 4,000 years of history and had to extend the mission of goodness to fight against evil once again. We know that this has manifested in the 2,000 years of history since Jesus. From this perspective, Jesus, who came to this earth, looked for the nation, the people, the tribe, the family, and the true family and brothers who could be governed by goodness. But were there any true families and brothers who could receive Jesus, the nation, and the people he was looking for? Here, history began to encounter a new problem. Today, countless Christians who believe in Jesus only know that he completed the providence of salvation on this earth. However, we must recognize that this is a great misunderstanding. When God established the people of Israel as the chosen people and nurtured them for 4,000 years, how much effort did He put in to establish them on the foundation of victory? The people of Israel were to unite with the Messiah from the day he arrived and defeat national and global evil to create a good world. How much did God desire in His heart for such a world to be realized through the people of Israel? How much did He hope that His will would be fulfilled when He sent His son? Yet, Jesus came to this earth and could not stand in that position, but instead carried the cross. Was this truly God's hope? No. If Jesus could save all people by dying on the cross, why would God have established the chosen people? Not a single person among the people of Israel, who had been nurtured with such effort, received Jesus, despite having grown on the historical foundation of victory over 4,000 years. The rulers of that nation, the very ones responsible for its ideological domain, should have received Jesus. That was their responsibility, yet they hurried to label him a heretic and obstruct his path. We cannot deny this historical fact. 

The Price Paid by the People of Israel for Killing Jesus Until Jesus came, when they suffered, God saved them, and when they were in lonely places, He protected them. God has made countless efforts. However, since Jesus came and went, the people of Israel have become a nation that is isolated in the world, and whenever revolutions occur, the blame often falls on the people of Israel. They have become a nation rejected by history and have become sacrificial offerings everywhere in the world. We know from history that the people of Israel had to pay the price for killing Jesus. But that was not the end. During World War II, they faced the blood price of six million being slaughtered by Hitler. How did such a sorrowful history arise? It was because they killed the sovereign of goodness who could resolve the overall will of God. We must understand that their sorrowful history is the blood price for killing Jesus. After killing Jesus, the people of Israel have lived as a nation without a country for so long, which, according to God's principle of indemnity, is a necessary disposition. This is not a reward that the chosen people should receive, but rather a punishment and curse that they must bear. We must clearly understand that. Who recognized the heart of Jesus, who had to bear the historical burden and fulfill the mission of the age? No one recognized him. Here, you must understand the connection of family. God sent Jesus through the family of Joseph, which was the family chosen by God among all of Israel. Through the family of Joseph, God's love was meant to connect with all of Israel, and thus God established the family of Joseph as a representative family of all of Israel.
22   What is a family? Then why did God love the unfortunate family of Joseph the most? It is because God sent His most beloved Son to that family. Therefore, the family of Joseph had to protect that Son and accept His entire will as their own. From this perspective, Jesus was born into the family of Joseph. He was born through the Holy Spirit from the body of the betrothed Mary. Who understood the desires and feelings of Jesus? Then what was the original hope of Jesus? Was it to choose disciples? Or was it to go through the past? Or was it to perform the miracle of feeding over five thousand people with five loaves and two fish? No. The hope of Jesus was to save the suffering Israelite nation from Roman oppression and to unify the world into a world of goodness at that time. That was the hope of Jesus who came as the Messiah. Nevertheless, at that time, there was no one who believed in Jesus as the Messiah or recognized Him as such. Who should the Israelite nation have been directly connected to at that time? Should they have been swept away by Roman policies? Or should they have been swayed by the social trends of that era? Neither. The one conclusion that the chosen people of Israel and Judaism should have reached was to become one with the Messiah. They had to unite with the Messiah, who held the purpose entrusted to Him, and establish a unified nation from an absolute standpoint to confront Rome. In doing so, they had to integrate with Rome and the entire world to build a global landscape centered around the Mediterranean. If the Israelite nation had done this at that time, the world would not have become what it is today. The apostles that Jesus desired were not foolish apostles who followed the evils of the world. However, the apostles who followed Jesus were not like that, so you should consider how miserable Jesus must have felt at that time. Jesus did not want foolish apostles. If the apostles that Jesus desired had been found, Israel could have overcome the world of evil. They could have overcome the forces of evil. Because Jesus bore the historical responsibility to establish a good world, His greatest wish was to defeat evil. Therefore, Jesus lived each day with this wish in mind, biting His tongue and holding on. This was something that no one at that time knew. The purpose of Jesus was to save all people, not to save individuals by dying on the cross. Then why was Jesus's purpose to save the world not fulfilled? Why was the temporary salvation of the nation not achieved? It was because the people who followed Jesus at that time did not realize that His wish was to save families, tribes, and the world all at once. Everyone only thought about believing in Jesus and going to heaven, without considering the wish that Jesus had. So how anxious must Jesus have been, who held in His heart the will of God to save the Israelite nation from Rome all at once? However, the apostles who followed Jesus did not know this. Even Peter did not know this. Who understood the heart of Jesus? Who knew the inner feelings of Jesus, who appealed to God every time He walked through the valley of the Mount of Olives? How much did Jesus want to tear down the power of Rome! Not the groups of Judaism and the Israelite nation that opposed Him and did not recognize Him, but the true Judaism and true Israel that could solemnly offer sacrifices before God were what Jesus longed for in His heart! The disciples did not even dream of such things. We must clearly understand that Jesus could not be satisfied with disciples who merely wished to believe and go to heaven. Such groups should not have become Jesus's disciples. Jesus came to this earth to unite with the rulers of the Jewish nation and the leaders of the Jewish sect responsible for the ideological field of that nation to make Rome submit before God. Even though the Israelite nation and Judaism had to unite and present the Messiah, they opposed Jesus instead. What would become of their fate? It is unreasonable that the chosen people opposed Jesus. 

23   Did Jesus come to die? Was His dream to die? Today's ignorant Christians might think so, but we must clearly understand that this is not the case. If Jesus came to die, why would God establish the chosen people? Could such a thing have been done at once? No. The family of Joseph was the family chosen by God. The family of John the Baptist was also a relative of the family of Joseph. Joseph was a descendant of David, whom God could not help but love. Therefore, God established the family of Joseph as the representative family of the nation. In doing so, He gave birth to Jesus alone. Then you must understand why Jesus had to leave the family of Joseph to choose His disciples. Jesus was born into this world in miserable circumstances. This was because Mary and Joseph did not fulfill their responsibilities. I will omit the details due to time constraints. From the day He was born, Jesus had to establish the law of loyalty before God so that He could first serve God and prepare a foundation to fulfill God's will. Where did this foundation need to be prepared? It had to be prepared from the family of Joseph. Of course, this is not recorded in the Bible. However, Jesus had to prepare it from the family of Joseph. Mary, who gave birth to Jesus, also knew how her son would turn out under the guidance of the beautiful angels of heaven. However, this does not mean that God was always with Mary while Jesus was growing up. Therefore, as time passed, Mary began to think that Jesus was born by chance. Jesus grew up in such a family of Joseph. 

24   Meanwhile, Joseph began to have doubts about whether Jesus was truly conceived by the Holy Spirit or by someone else. The more he thought about it, the more troubled he became. Think about it! How would Joseph's heart have felt when his betrothed brought home a child and said it was conceived by the Holy Spirit? He may have believed the fact that God taught him, but every time he looked at Jesus or Mary, how could he not feel intense pain? Thus, Jesus could not help but grow up sorrowfully in the arms of a stepfather. You must understand the circumstances of Jesus. He was a sorrowful Jesus. He served his younger siblings but had never received service from them. Even when Jesus heard something from Joseph, He could not truly hear it from the position of receiving a father's love. He heard it from the position of being suspected by a stepfather. In this way, Jesus grew up in invisible abuse. Jesus, who had many sorrows, even when Mary had an unpleasant experience with Joseph or if Joseph frowned even a little, could not help but think while looking at Jesus. What do you think? Can you truly understand the feelings of such a person? If a woman who remarried with a stepchild had a husband who frowned even a little, how could she not relate everything to her stepchild? You must understand that Jesus was in a position where He could not have a foundation of happiness. That is why there was much sorrow in Jesus's heart. As the holidays approached, His younger siblings could rejoice and prepare with their parents, but Jesus, who had many thoughts, could not ask for even one piece of clothing without being cautious. Therefore, Jesus could not help but face the holidays with a miserable appearance. Such things are not in the Bible. Then how do I know this? You can know this by asking Jesus. Think about it. Even if there were rice cakes prepared at home for the holidays, Jesus could not reach out first and say, “Mother, please give me some!” Even when there was something good, even while looking at the beautiful clothes that His younger siblings wore, Jesus could not say, “Please give me some. Please do something for me.” You must understand that Jesus was someone who could not express all of these circumstances! Jesus, who could not enjoy days with friends of his age, could not align himself with the environment! Thinking of such things breaks my heart. Who knows these things? People only know, “Oh! The King of kings, the only begotten Son of God has come to this earth!” They do not know that Jesus, as a child, shed endless tears every time he looked at children joyfully celebrating the holidays with their parents. As He looked around the world, what He longed for was the love of parents who could embrace Him. Jesus, who had a younger sibling, could not even call him a younger brother! Jesus was in a position where He could not declare himself as an older brother in front of those siblings! He truly lived a miserable life. You must understand these circumstances of Jesus. Everyone, think quietly. Is this something that Teacher Moon made up or not? Would you agree? Could God have taught them every day, saying, “You rascal, you rascal!”? You must understand that Jesus was sorrowful because it was not possible. “The foxes have holes, and the birds of the air have nests, but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay His head.” (Matt 8:20) Do you know what this means? It means He was like this from birth. Do you know why Jesus said, “Who is my mother, and who are my brothers? … For whoever does the will of my Father in heaven is my brother and sister and mother”? (Matt 12:48-50) You must understand that Jesus went with a heart full of unutterable sorrow.

27   Jesus felt the responsibility for the salvation of humanity and secretly devoted Himself. Jesus grew up in the home of a carpenter. He worked as an assistant under Joseph, the carpenter. However, every time Jesus held a sickle, carved wood, or planed wood, He worked with the heart to save Israel. He worked with the solemn responsibility that the chosen people of Israel should not be like this, and that He would carve and shape them to create a new Israel. With this heart, He always embraced and loved Israel, working with a heart that could turn back to God. No one knew the wish of Jesus, who held such a thought. However, Jesus devoted Himself to preparing His life while consulting with God. On quiet nights when His parents and siblings were asleep, unaware of anything, He would go outside, gaze at the stars in the sky, appeal to His heart, look at the flowing river, or the leaves swaying in the wind, and comfort Himself, saying, “You know my circumstances and understand my wishes, right?” Although humans did not know Jesus, all things and nature became His friends. Jesus, who came to this earth for humanity and needed to be recognized by humans, could not find true humans or an environment where true humans could live, which made Him long for the embrace of nature and the embrace of God. You must understand that this was Jesus. Originally, if Joseph and Mary had known that Jesus was the true Son sent by God, the Prince of God, and the Messiah for all people, they should have honored Him as the Prince of God from the day He was born. They should have worshiped Jesus every day. Because He is the King of kings and has come as the sovereign of heaven who can rule the entire universe for eternity, from the day Jesus was born, Joseph and Mary should have devoted themselves to Him with all their hearts and fulfilled their duties of loyalty. From a human perspective, is there any law that says one must fulfill their duties of loyalty before their own son? However, according to heavenly law, that is how it should be. Originally, when God sent Jesus to the family of Joseph, it was not to make Him suffer. God had taught in advance and caused Jesus to be born through Mary's womb, not to make Him suffer, but to ensure that He would receive glory and protection, not to be chased and persecuted. However, it began to go wrong from the family of Joseph. The more Jesus realized that He bore the heavenly mission upon Himself, the more He struggled to lead His siblings and parents before God's will. The words, “How often would I have gathered your children together as a hen gathers her chicks under her wings!” (Matt 23:37) were not spoken about the Israelite nation. They were spoken about His own family. Jesus first worked hard for His own family. Jesus, who came with the responsibility to establish the kingdom of God on behalf of the heavenly principles, wanted to give first to His closest beloved parents. Wouldn't that be the case, everyone? If there is something good, isn't it a child's duty to want to give it first to their beloved parents? And wouldn't they want to give it first to their beloved siblings and relatives? That is why, from the time Jesus became aware, He thought about the historical connection of God visiting the family of Joseph and prayed many times to establish God's will centered on the family of Joseph. But did Joseph and Mary honor Jesus? The principle is that even when serving meals, they should serve Jesus first. Joseph and Mary should have been responsible for Jesus's entire life. Shouldn't it be that way? If we look at it centered on the will, it should be that way.
29 So Joseph had to take care of Jesus. Joseph had to become the chief disciple among the disciples. Do you believe that Joseph had to be Jesus' chief disciple? What do you think you would have done if you were in such a situation? Think about it. Would you have done it or not? Jesus, who had to abandon the foundation prepared by God, wanted to fulfill the great and tremendous mission He received from God starting from Joseph's family. This was because there was a principled reason for it. Joseph had to be Jesus' chief disciple. If that happened, would Jesus' siblings follow or not? Although it is not written in the Bible, it is said that if the siblings wished for their older brother to appear as the Messiah, they criticized Him for not going to the many people in Jerusalem. Would it have been okay for the siblings to criticize like that? It is also said that Mary looked down on Jesus. She did not treat Him normally. However, fundamentally, it had to be fulfilled starting from that household. It was necessary to fulfill God's will centered on Joseph's family. Then, who is John the Baptist? He is Jesus' cousin. They are relatives. The relatives had to unite centered on Joseph's family. Joseph and Mary had to unite to uphold Jesus' will, and the siblings had to become disciples, and all the relatives had to become apostles, meaning that the siblings and relatives had to become the 12 disciples, 70 disciples, and 120 disciples to overcome the evil world. If this had been done and confronted other races and nations, you must understand that Jesus would never have been crucified. However, the will of Jesus, which had to be fulfilled starting from the family, could not be realized. (Matthew 12:50), this means that His mother and siblings did not do God's will. You must understand this clearly. Did Jesus come to die? No. He was the one who was wronged. To indemnify what God had worked hard for 4,000 years to establish Joseph's family, Jesus had to negotiate with God. That is why there was a 40-day fasting period. For this reason, after 40 days, Jesus entered the second course. You must understand how the second course began. What do you think the heart of Jesus was like while walking this second course? In this way, it was necessary to create an environment where the Israelite people and Judaism would have to follow. However, all of this collapsed. Because everything collapsed, a direct confrontation began. The intention was to first fulfill the will at the family level and then face the nation, but instead, they faced the nation and came out to find the family. Do you understand what I mean? It should have been addressed in the order of individual, family, tribe, nation, and state, but because this was broken, it had to be restored in reverse. Therefore, it was necessary to go out to find the nation, to find the denomination, and to organize tribes among the nation and denomination, and to reorganize families and find the connections with parents and siblings. 4) The history of humanity is the history of restoration providence.  
We know that the history of fallen humanity is the history of humans walking the path of restoration to return to their original position. Because of Adam's fall, God intended to carry out the restoration providence centered on the family of Adam through Cain and Abel. However, Cain killed Abel, and thus that intention was not fulfilled. Consequently, it extended through Noah, Abraham, Moses, and John the Baptist until the time of Jesus. The history of humanity, which has been extended due to disbelief and mistakes, meant that Jesus had to indemnify all historical failures. He had to set conditions to indemnify and restore the entire history, that is, the vertical historical path horizontally. It was Jesus' responsibility and mission to indemnify and restore from the individual and family level through the nation of Israel to the world. By the completion of Jesus alone, what was to be accomplished in the family of Adam would be fulfilled, everything that was to be accomplished in the families of Noah and Abraham would be fulfilled, the mission of Moses who led the nation of Israel would be completed, and even the mission of John the Baptist, who was to conclude the Old Testament history, would be fulfilled. This was the mission of Jesus. Therefore, the victory of Jesus alone brings the victory of all of Israel and the victory of the entire restoration history. This is what allows us to embark on the global path of returning to Canaan. However, due to the disbelief of the Jewish people, Jesus was unable to complete the overall mission of indemnification and restoration, and thus that intention was extended again, leading to the passage of 2,000 years of history until now. So what was Jesus' desire? Jesus' desire was to fulfill God's will on earth without bearing the cross. In other words, it was to redeem all of humanity and return them to Eden. Amen. <Message> The title of today’s message, ‘Victorious Subject,’ is what all fallen humanity desires, regardless of individuals, tribes, or nations, and it is what Heaven has long desired. The reason the noun ‘victory’ has come into existence is that our hope is to meet God, and God’s desire is to make us children of victory. If we cannot find a position like this title, we cannot bring about the fruits of God’s labor, and we know well that humanity’s hopes cannot be fulfilled. Before individuals become victorious subjects, it is impossible for groups, nations, or the world to become victorious subjects. We must understand that the word ‘victory’ originally did not apply to humans. After creating Adam and Eve, God blessed them to be fruitful and multiply, filling the earth with the authority of life and to govern all things on His behalf. They were to have the authority to govern the universe beyond the standard of life. This was the mission of the ancestors of humanity, yet they lost that mission. Therefore, we must understand that the term ‘victory’ has remained as an unavoidable noun on the path of restoration. We cannot become subjects without surpassing the standard of victory. We can only appear with the qualifications of a subject if we inevitably surpass the standard of victory. However, for the two characters of victory to be established, there must be an enemy to fight against. To achieve victory, we must go through the path of battle. Without going through the path of battle, we cannot bring about victory. Who is the target of this battle? It is undoubtedly Satan, the enemy of humanity and God. This Satan is the archangel Lucifer, who lured Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden. We know that this Satan has deprived us of the authority of victory for thousands of years while violating us, the descendants of Adam. Therefore, we cannot deny that we must remove this Satan, who has deprived us of the authority of victory, in order to establish the standard of victory. From the day humanity entered the fate of the Fall, we lost God’s love. We lost the original personality that God created. We lost the promised words that God gave us. The overall cause of losing these things lies with whom? Of course, there is a cause with Adam and Eve, but we know that the primary cause lies with Satan, the subject of evil. The opponent we must defeat is Satan. So, what is the ultimate issue in expelling this Satan? It is how to center around God’s love. We must manifest centered on God’s love. If we do not center on God’s love, we cannot become the subjects who govern Heaven and earth. We must understand that without commanding based on the truth of God, which is grounded in the principles of Heaven and earth, we cannot subdue this Satan. However, until now, humans have not become the personalities who can channel God’s heart or the protagonists of truth who can channel God’s personality. Therefore, we must seek the truth and establish a personality that can align with that truth, and that truth and personality must become one in order to embrace the universe and allow God’s love to be connected there. Thus, the history of humanity has been a history of pioneering truth. 
93 We must clearly understand that by pioneering the truth, subduing Satan through that truth, and receiving God’s love in a position where we have the authority to govern Satan as one with that truth, the position of a universal subject is determined. 6) Purpose of Judgment

7) Be on God's Side
<Summary of the Message> When I embarked on this path, I was a youth like you. When I received my mission from Jesus, the great question was how to fulfill that heavy responsibility. I realized that the strength of Noah, Abraham, and Moses to go the purposeful path was stronger than anyone else’s. On February 22, 1948, when the teacher went to Pyongyang prison, I thought there would be someone promised by God when viewed from the principle of a thousand miles, so I went with hope. A year prior, I felt an irresistible heart that I could not rebel against because heaven had taught me that I would come. The crack in the teacher's front tooth occurred when he was trying to make a needle in Hungnam prison. How precious that needle was! I realized that the person God seeks is just as precious. I enjoyed the mountains and trees, but sometimes I could not see the sun. There are three groups in the universe. They are the group belonging to God, the group belonging to Satan, and the group that belongs neither to God nor to Satan. You must find your fate among these three. To belong to God, you must achieve victory. The command to love your enemies means to love that person to detach them from Satan. Satan is an adulterer before God. And humanity is the child of that adulterer. Therefore, Satan is the enemy. Only those who are deeply committed to avenging this enemy can become people on God’s side. To be saved, one must first avenge the enemy. The base of this enemy extends from the world to my very cells. Because humans fell at the completion stage of growth, Satan occupies two-thirds of the entire path, and God operates within one-third. *
8) Let Us Become Sacrifices for the Nation
<Summary of the Message> Unifying democracy and communism is our mission. To achieve this, at least one person must be placed in each of the 2,400 districts nationwide. To form a triad, about 7,000 people are needed. These individuals must be college graduates or higher. Originally, we intended to focus on Ewha Womans University and Yonsei University, but that plan collapsed, and the direction changed. Thus, we shifted to focus on middle and high school students. The three-year period must show that this nation cannot do without unification believers. South Korea, with its current state, has no way to block the infiltration of communism. They infiltrate the lower classes. Therefore, we have been spreading the principles to local people and continuing lifestyle guidance and enlightenment movements. The triad in each district must be responsible for ideological guidance, lifestyle guidance, and enlightenment movements. Originally, ideological guidance should be the responsibility of the church, while lifestyle guidance and enlightenment movements should be the responsibility of the agricultural department, but when you go to the district, you must take responsibility for all three. If we send college students to the countryside for a year to take responsibility for middle school education, they will also gain an understanding of rural circumstances and develop patriotism. We must leave behind the true ideology of becoming sacrifices for the nation in the university. To do this, we must raise young people who can take on the responsibility of the judge. This is the purpose of founding this organization. *

157 <Message> The title of the message I would like to think about with you today is "Blessings Call." Blessings - the land that God and humanity desire. What was the original purpose of Jesus coming to this earth? It was, of course, to establish blessings. Not only Jesus, but also countless prophets, sages, and heroes throughout history who came with a purpose and left traces on this earth all came to find the right path to seek blessings. We acknowledge that culture and history have been built upon the achievements of such saints and sages. And now we are living within the social sphere of that cultural realm. So, what is the overall goal that today’s society, nation, and world are striving for? It cannot be denied that it is also heading towards blessings. Whether big or small, whether a large country or a small one, or whether it is an advanced nation boasting authority in its time or a backward nation with a miserable fate, everyone is struggling to reach the goal of seeking blessings. Throughout the many difficult paths of history, countless people have struggled to find blessings, but we have yet to meet anyone who claims to have found blessings that all of humanity universally desires or who has lived in such a place. Far from meeting such people, there has not even been a group that has raised a global call to construct blessings. Moreover, no one knows that blessings will be established in this world and that the day will come when we will live there. When we think about this, it is of utmost importance for us to understand what kind of life leads us to blessings and how we connect the issues of our life and death, reality, and future to blessings. If God had a solemn hope and ideology when He created this earth and human ancestors at the beginning, what would that have been? It would have been to live in a world of blessings. The ideology of blessings is the ideology that God had before the creation and the ideology He intended to establish at the time of creation. It was also the ideology that God, who has been providentially guiding history after the fall, had to restore humanity. When we think about the fact that God is behind history, we must recognize how much effort humanity has made to achieve blessings and how much God has strived for it. 
158   Humanity lost blessings due to the fall. God created Adam and hoped that the entire earth would unite with heaven, that God could not be absent, and that evil could not exist, thus becoming an eternal world of blessings. However, Adam fell during the process of pioneering the path of blessings, creating a sorrowful day, and since then, this world has fallen away from the original world it was meant to be. We cannot deny this fact. So, who was the one who lost blessings? It was our ancestors, Adam and Eve. You must understand that they fell. The important issue we must first resolve is how to return to the state Adam was in before the fall in order to find blessings again. To resolve this, we must understand the motivation behind Adam's loss of blessings. He did not believe God's word. He could not become a representative who could stand in place of God's word. Furthermore, he could not become a subject of heart who could embrace the universe from the position of the protagonist of blessings on behalf of God. We understand that this is what the fall is. Losing the true words of God that could establish a new law, failing to become someone who could keep, follow, and act according to that law, and failing to become the true protagonist of love who could govern the universe centered on that law is what the fall is. 
159   Because humanity lost the world of blessings due to the fall, countless figures throughout history have struggled and died to pioneer blessings, and history has unfolded as a history of bloody struggles until now, which we cannot deny. Adam was the total responsible person who was to sing happiness with God in blessings, valuing everything in heaven and earth like God and governing the created world on behalf of God. However, Adam failed to establish a position of unity with God, who created the world. That is the fall. We must understand that God has been striving since the day Adam fell to restore all of that. God, who should have called Adam with a hopeful heart from the position of fulfillment, had to call him from a sorrowful place where He could not fulfill His purpose. The day He called, "Adam! Adam!" was not a day to welcome Adam with joy. That day was the day blessings were lost, the day his personality was shattered, and the day the fortunes of heaven and earth were turned upside down. The word that God cried out with a sorrowful heart that day was, "Adam, where are you?" From that day on, God came out to find the lost blessings again. God left the name of blessings for the future and has been working through historical paths to achieve those blessings until now. On the sorrowful day Adam fell, God cried out in grief with the words, "Adam, where are you?" This was a lamentation and a cry that arose from the sorrow of losing blessings. How could God not be sorrowful and lament when facing Adam, who realized and confessed that his actions had betrayed the heavenly principles? We must once again feel God's sorrow. 
160   Therefore, for 6,000 years after Adam, God has run forth with a heartfelt desire to restore blessings, but humanity has been unable to unite before God's cries for the blessings He desires and could not find that path together. We must understand that this has also become God's sorrow and frustration. Forgetting the mission, God called Abraham to walk the path of restoration. The voice calling, "Abraham!" was not just calling one person. It was a cry that carried the heart of grievance that had been felt since Adam's time, seeking to find the blessings that had been lost, and at the same time, it was a voice calling forth the new owner of blessings, a voice to establish a family of blessings, a nation of blessings, and a world of blessings. However, Abraham, who bore the responsibility, did not realize that God's voice was a cry for blessings and a cry for the historical miseries to be resolved. The moment Abraham placed the offering on the altar was a moment of promise to establish the world of blessings and a decisive moment to resolve historical grievances. Yet, Abraham did not understand the true meaning of God's command to offer sacrifices, nor did he realize how precious the heavenly mission he had to bear was, and centered only on his own position, he offered sacrifices. Therefore, the act of not dividing the offering became a motive for God's sorrow again and later became the motive for Jesus' crucifixion, which we have learned through the principles. Abraham, who was called by God, was to manifest as a new prophet and ancestor who could govern the blessings of the dawn. However, when Abraham appeared before God, who was crying out for blessings, he did not have the attitude and character to bear all of that. We must once again reflect on this as a historical grievance.
161 Abraham had forgotten that he had the responsibility to establish a just law that could judge history and the times, and to build the world of future desires. Who would have thought that a small, uncut offering from Abraham would become the origin that disrupts the course of history? God came to Abraham, hoping for the day when the grief bound by Adam would be resolved through him, but once again found Himself in the position of having to call Abraham with a sad heart. Therefore, God commanded Abraham to offer his only son Isaac as a sacrifice. Who could have known the sorrowful situation of such a father? God's hope for the Israelite people, who were suffering in Egypt, was that they would not have to walk the troubled path from Noah to Abraham again, which is why they had to endure 400 years of sorrowful suffering in Egypt. The mistakes of those whom God called, that is, those who were to bear the responsibility of the times and the providence of the age, do not end with individual mistakes. They involve the overall issues of history, the entire era, and all future problems. However, neither Abraham himself nor the Israelite people were aware of this fact. They did not realize that, as the heavenly vanguard bearing the mission of pioneers, they had a responsibility to fulfill. Four thousand years ago, Egypt had a highly developed culture. The Israelite people entered such Egypt and lived in suffering for 400 years, and you must understand what God desired from them. God did not want them to simply end up as laborers who toiled in slavery, making bricks. The greater the grief, the greater the resentment, the more God wanted them to become those who resolved to trample upon the stronghold of their enemies. This was the life of the Israelite people who forgot God's heart. 

162 Welfare calls. The Israelite people had to have the spirit to say to the Egyptian officials who wielded whips over them, "One day, we will wield the whip against you. Although you are currently boasting about your culture to the world, one day we will establish a new culture that can trample upon that culture." They needed to be equipped with the greatest internal foundation. If they had done so, Israel's welfare and Canaan's welfare would have welcomed them, and there would have been no lingering grievances in history. The mistakes of Abraham as an individual should have been compensated by the entire Israelite nation, and they should have emerged with a strong ideological conviction to trample upon the stronghold of historical enemies. The Israelite people, who worshiped nature gods and sun gods, lost the spiritual foundation necessary to rise above the culture of Egypt and establish a new history and culture centered on the ideology of Judaism. Their desire ended merely in fleeing from Egypt to return to the welfare of Canaan. Canaan's welfare was calling. It was calling the Israelite people. However, it was not calling those who wanted to escape from the suffering of Egypt. It was calling a nation that could take revenge on the suffering of Egypt and rise above the cultural realm of their enemies. Today, our nation must also ignite the courage to step forward when the path of death approaches. Thus, we must embrace the grievances passed down from our ancestors and boldly decide to become the heroes for the establishment of a new Israel, moving toward the places that God commands and ordains. A nation lacking such a conviction will only face devastation, misery, division, and destruction. This is a historical fact. Why did God allow the Israelite people to suffer for 400 years? It was to enable them to establish a culture greater than that of Egypt and to have authority greater than that of the Egyptian people. However, the Israelite people, who did not understand God's original intention, could not avoid going astray.

163 The Israelite people were to create a new culture and a chosen people's rights, and through this era, they encountered the times of King Saul, King David, and King Solomon. Saul was raised before God and received solemn commands. Because he bore the mission as the representative of the founding of Israel, he could not go out only for his personal happiness. The greater the authority of the foreign nations scattered in the world of enemies, the more they had to become a nation equipped with greater authority to rise above it. Thus, they had to create a culture that surpassed the Roman culture of the time and establish that tradition. He also had to gather the scattered people, unify them, crush the enemies, and establish the rights of the chosen people capable of creating a new culture centered on a new ideology. To fulfill such a mission, he had to be filled with righteous indignation and resolve to alleviate historical grievances, but the steps taken by Saul and the Israelite people deviated from what God desired. Therefore, they moved toward a sorrowful path that left behind a history filled with grievances. David, too, should not have been satisfied merely with ascending to the throne; he had to establish a nation that could rise above Rome based on his kingship and build a national culture. When conquering foreign nations, he had to completely cut off their cultures without exception. Thus, he had to rise above Rome and wield the sword of truth before the enemies who had caused grievances for countless generations. This was the responsibility of Saul, David, and Solomon, but they failed to fulfill it. Although Solomon is praised as a figure who could glorify God in history, he was Solomon within the confines of his time, not the Solomon who could be praised beyond that era. The one who can be called by welfare, the one who can be the master of welfare, is not the one who sings of happiness in that time. He must rise above the history of that time and establish a new culture, commanding humanity to move toward that world.

164 Welfare calls. This was Solomon's responsibility. Solomon built the temple for offerings and gathered the patriarchs of Israel within that temple to boast of his kingship. Solomon's authority had to break and shatter all traces of cultures established by countless nations up to that time, removing all cultures formed through the connections of fallen races to establish a new culture. However, Solomon forgot this. Therefore, God's intention to be realized through Solomon could not help but shift toward those who were carrying such hopes. God has been advising through prophets and seers over thousands of years of historical progress. This was a call for the Israelite people to fulfill their national mission. Does the world know how to surrender before the Israelite people? They were given the mission to move toward welfare, so if there is opposition in front of that path, they were to overcome it. Why did God send Jesus to this earth? It was to resolve the grievances of seeking welfare, to alleviate the grievances of not living in welfare, and to heal God's grievances of not being praised in glory due to the loss of welfare. This was the mission of Jesus. In the Bible, there are many scenes where Jesus is crowded by the masses in the Jerusalem temple, entering into unjust situations. Seeing this, today’s Christians believe as if the suffering from the Garden of Gethsemane to the summit of Golgotha was natural, and they believe that Jesus came to be crucified. If that is the case, I think such a Jesus is unnecessary. Jesus should have been the one who could establish welfare and remove the culture of enemies to create a new cultural world, but due to the disbelief of the Jewish people, he could not become that Jesus. Because of this, Christians were persecuted in Rome for 400 years, and for the past 2,000 years, countless ancestors and forebears of faith have been executed. Yet, they worked with blood, sweat, and tears toward a single goal that heaven aims for. Even on the path of death, they cried out earnestly, "O God, let welfare be realized on this earth. Let the protagonist of welfare appear." This is the Christianity that has continued to connect the cries of grievances, rebuilding hope every time the altar of heaven collapses. Thus, today’s 20th-century Christian cultural world has been established. Will history end with this? No. Even now, democracy centered on Christian thought has not achieved welfare. Likewise, communism has not yet achieved welfare centered on its ideology. The welfare that all humanity desires cannot be achieved through the current democratic culture or communist culture. So how will welfare be achieved? A new culture must be created. When I visited America last time, I looked around the culture of today established on the basis of democratic thought and thought, "This is the center headquarters that can command the whole world. The new cultural world to be established in the future must be a world that can rise above this." I prayed for that. Why do we boast of the Empire State Building? It may be a point of pride for a passing era, but it cannot serve as a signpost or a tower in establishing a new world. You must understand that God's desire to establish a new world and a new history centered on a new culture of welfare is at a higher level than that.

11) Day of Hopeful Parents
As you know, today is Parents' Day. Centered around March 1960, we set a new day that had never existed in history, and that day is Parents' Day. This day must be welcomed with joy from heaven and earth. The days lost due to the fall—if our ancestors Adam and Eve had not fallen, we would have already celebrated Parents' Day. However, because Adam and Eve fell, true parents must first come to this earth for us to celebrate Parents' Day. Only then can we celebrate Children's Day after having children born from the True Parents based on that day. When that happens, we will also be able to celebrate the day when we can govern all creation. God promised such days to the unfallen human ancestors. However, due to the fall of human ancestors, we have been unable to celebrate Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Creation, which were the ideal of God's creation. Therefore, God, as the one who has completed the purpose of creation, could rejoice on March 22, 1966 (Tuesday) at 10 a.m., at the headquarters church. * These words were spoken at the 7th Parents' Day (Lunar March 1) commemorative ceremony and were compiled from issues of <Seonghwa> No. 54 (April 1, 1966), No. 55 (May 1, 1966), No. 56 (June 1, 1966), No. 58 (August 1966), No. 59 (September 1966), and No. 61 (December 1966), with the title added by the editor.

178 The Day of Hopeful Parents has not been a day we could boast about. Of course, the fall of Adam and Eve was the state of losing God, but because of their fall, God also lost Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Creation. Thus, God lost all the days He hoped for. Among the days God hoped for were the day when there are parents in the created world, the day when there is a family centered around those parents, and the day when there is one tribe, nation, and world centered around that family. However, without being able to celebrate those glorious days, the history of humanity has been woven into a history of the fall, becoming an evil world, evil nations, evil peoples, evil tribes, evil families, and evil individuals. These are not the original purpose of creation that God hoped for, so God will not leave them as they are. Then who is the culprit that created such evil? It is Satan. Therefore, we must restore this satanic world back to God's side. We must establish the world that God desires. To do this, we must fight to uplift the evil world, and we must ascend to the good world in contrast to how Satan established the evil world. That is why God has carried out the providence of salvation through three stages over 6,000 years of history. Thus, we have passed through the age of servants in the Old Testament and the age of adopted children in the New Testament, arriving at the age of the covenant. In the age of the covenant, children must appear to prepare a place for parents and must serve the parents. Until now, God has been carrying out this restoration history. 

The Savior as a Parent
The ultimate purpose of Jesus, who came to this earth 2,000 years ago, was not to save servants. It was not to save adopted children either. Then what purpose did Jesus come for? He came with the highest purpose of saving all created beings, coming as a Savior with the heart of a parent. If someone you truly love fell into the water, you would want to save them first. If a beloved son fell into the water, which parent would send a servant to save their son? If there is such a parent, that parent would not truly love their son. Likewise, if a parent had a youngest son who fell into the water and sent his older brother to save him, that parent would also not be a loving parent. Such parents do not exist. From the perspective of God's heart, what kind of Savior does the fallen humanity, in a state like drowning, need? They need a Savior as a parent. If God truly loves fallen humanity, from what position would He want to save them? God wants to save humanity from the position of a parent. This is also the reason why God established the Messiah on this earth to carry out the providence of salvation. Therefore, before Jesus began his three-year public ministry in Nazareth, what did he need to have? It was the position of a parent. He needed to become Jesus as the Messiah. He was not a being who represented the Messiah. Thus, you must understand that he had to first establish the position of a parent. He had to become the true ancestor for humanity, the true parent. However, because he could not become the true parent, those born until today with the bloodline of false parents have not been able to connect with the True Parents and have never experienced the love of the True Parents. Just like Jesus, who had to find a bride first, God cannot establish those who are born of different bloodlines, that is, those who have not passed through the bloodline of the True Parents, as direct children. Because the bloodline that must face God is connected to a bloodline that God does not desire, no matter how much effort and sincerity humans put in, when they go before God, they can only become adopted children, not true sons and daughters. It is a sorrowful story. That is why, as recorded in Romans, we can only call God ‘Abba Father’ in the name of adopted children, and that too has been made possible because of Jesus. Although Jesus has already come and gone, when many people today receive salvation, the highest standard can only be that of an adopted child. Then what is an adopted child? An adopted child is one who has a different bloodline. Having lost the True Parents and connected with false parents, unless the root is cut off, one cannot become a true son. Therefore, after 4,000 years of history following the fall, Jesus came. To be born again, there must be parents. Without parents, one cannot give birth to children. That is why God sent Jesus as the Messiah to this earth. So what did Jesus have to do when he came? He had to become the True Parent to save the countless humans living on this earth. To do this, he had to find a bride. The twelve disciples were not the issue. He had to find a bride first. However, after walking the paths of the first, second, and third stages, because Jesus could not find a bride, he had no choice but to set the twelve apostles in the position of children. This content is not found in the Bible. To save humanity and to give birth to humanity again, Jesus had to find a bride. He needed the Holy Spirit. That is why Jesus said to Nicodemus, “Unless one is born again, he cannot see the kingdom of God.” (John 3:3) To this, Nicodemus replied, “How can a man be born when he is old? Can he enter a second time into his mother's womb and be born?” (John 3:4) Then Jesus lamented, “Are you the teacher of Israel, and do not know these things?” (John 3:10). Humanity must be born again centered on Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Since Satan has taken everything away, humanity must be born again centered on God. Without being reborn through the bloodline of the True Parents and establishing a heartistic foundation, one cannot stand before the heavenly principles. Therefore, Jesus had to establish a principled foundation, that is, the foundation of parents. To become a parent, he had to first find and establish a bride. It was not the purpose to find the twelve disciples. However, that got reversed. Thus, it required hundreds of times more effort. Who is Jesus? He is the Second Adam who came in place of Adam. That is why he had to find the bride, Eve. Only then could he restore the lost position of parents. He had to find someone who could work together for God to restore what was lost. 

The Mission of the Bride
The man represents heaven, and the woman represents the earth. Jesus came as the bridegroom representing all men, so he had to find a bride. However, the Israelites at the time did not understand Jesus' will. The disciples also could not cooperate because they did not understand this will. Originally, this was to be accomplished in the family of Joseph, but because it could not be done, Jesus could not become the True Parent. The family of Joseph had to realize that God had blessed his family after 4,000 years of providence and had to fulfill that responsibility with a sense of total responsibility for the times. Moreover, it was Jesus' mission to find and fulfill God's will through the family of Joseph. Therefore, Jesus questioned his parents three times. However, his parents, who did not understand the will, ultimately could not comprehend Jesus' will. Thus, Jesus was betrayed by his family and lost his family. Having become such, Jesus had to create a new family to fulfill God's will. When even the Israelite nation did not believe in Jesus, he could not unfold his will in the family of Joseph and the nation of Judah, and he was pursued and chased by them. That is why God took Jesus away. Jesus had to find a bride on this earth and establish the connection of True Parents to set the Day of Parents before the world and God. However, what would have been Jesus' heart when he left this world without fulfilling that will? Today, we must understand this. According to the principle of indemnity and restoration, parents must come forth. If at that time Jesus had sought a bride from the position of a bachelor, how wonderful would that have been? However, Jesus came from a position where he could not fulfill the stages of restoration that needed to be accomplished—rebirth, growth, and perfection—so he had to lay the foundation of victory by overcoming all of this. In establishing the foundation of victory both internally and externally, he had to first settle the sins through the opposite path that had fallen because of Eve. To do this, Jesus had to prepare the bridal chamber and find a bride. Nevertheless, because he could not do this, Jesus fasted and prayed. This became God's sorrow and Jesus' sorrow. Because saving humanity was the hope and purpose, Jesus, who left without fulfilling that will, must return. Then what must Jesus do first when he returns? It is not to meet the disciples. He must find a bride. This bride is the Christian community that has been waiting and preparing for the bridegroom to come in the position of the bride on behalf of all humanity. Because the Israelite nation could not fulfill their responsibility toward Jesus, the 4,000 years of history was extended by 2,000 years, and humanity had to walk the path of global indemnity once again. This path is also a path of preparing the foundation of a global bride, so the Lord who is to come again must find a bride. Jesus came to this earth as the Second Adam. The Holy Spirit also came to this earth but could not take on the body of a bride. If you go to the spirit world, the Holy Spirit is the Mother God. When Jesus establishes the reality on this earth, the bride must know all the contents of the heavenly principles and, thus, fulfill the qualifications of a bride in the truth, waiting for the Messiah to come as a bride and preparing to welcome him. Therefore, one family must be prepared, one nation must be prepared, and the world must be prepared. This is the responsibility of the bride. That is why, entering the 1960s, the women's movement is being launched globally. Women must solve what men cannot solve. Even if there are many people on this earth, all are fallen descendants born with the bloodline of evil.

184 Parents' Day of hope. However, not everyone can become a bride. Not everyone who participates in a marathon can come in first place. Then, among the many candidates for brides, whom does God choose? He comes to find those who welcome the Lord. What is a bride? I find the term "bride" unpleasant. The term "bride" arose because of the fall. It exists because of the fall. If there had been no fall, the term "bride" would not be necessary. 12) Suffer in the Same Position as the Teacher
<Summary of Words> April 3rd was an unforgettable trial day for the Teacher. Due to the jealousy of established Christian denominations and the religious extermination policy of the communist authorities, the Teacher was detained at the Ministry of Internal Affairs on February 22nd and had his head shaved on February 25th. A religious trial under communist rule is unthinkable. That day (April 3rd) was the day that marked 40 days since his detention. What I still cannot forget is the scene of comrades being tortured. If the Teacher confessed, more people would suffer. The scene of comrades being tortured is the most painful and unforgettable. It is sorrowful that those who suffered so much have not remained before heaven. From God's perspective, the suffering of those comrades must have been more sorrowful than that of Jesus. The reason Christianity has developed is also because it has tried to stand in a position of suffering more than God. After Jesus died, many were prepared for death, but when Jesus was alive, no one was. The Teacher is concerned about what to leave behind. He wishes to establish a tradition of shedding tears together with God and walking the path of death. April 3, 1966, Sunday, at the former headquarters church. * These words were spoken after the report meeting of the Earth District and are compiled from notes taken by former president Yoo Yong-won. The title was added by the editor.

202 Suffer in the Same Position as the Teacher

The reason God cannot abandon the Israelite people is precisely because of this heart. The Teacher is grateful that he is still alive and can carry out heavenly work.

13) Let Us Participate with Faith and Ability
<Summary of Words> When the Teacher first received his mission and started on the path of the will, he thought he must overcome the hill where the cells cry out.
