Because he set out with such determination, he did not lose heart even while wearing shackles. During the Japanese occupation, the Japanese were the enemy, and when he was in the North, the communists were the enemy. Moreover, he still feels resentment for being opposed even by Christians. This must be resolved. He thought of Joseph, who was sold into Egypt. The people who had sworn tears together would ask him when they saw him walking a difficult path, "Are you still walking that path?" He would show them a day when they could weep. He would make it happen. An old friend he met next to the prison door laughed and said, "Things have turned out well." He would make them weep and writhe. When he suffered such cruel torture from the communists, he swore before God that he would overcome this difficulty. If he is opposed by individuals, will he take revenge on those individuals? No. Behind them is Satan. That Satan must be expelled from this earth. May 1, 1966, Sunday, noon, Taereung. * These words were spoken during the 12th anniversary ceremony of the association held at Taereung and are compiled from the publication "Seonghwa," No. 55 (dated May 1, 1966). 16) Indemnity Restoration and the Responsibility of the Family
<Summary of Words> Originally, there should not have been terms like restoration or indemnity in the human world. However, because human ancestors took the wrong path, the terms restoration and indemnity became necessary. The term restoration carries the meaning of pursuing the standard of truth. Indemnity restoration begins from the lowest standard. Humans rise using their hearts as a stepping stone. In other words, they return through the age of servants to the age of sons and daughters. In restoring each of these ages, there is always a standard, that is, a center that is determined and crossed over. In the age of servants, a true servant's standard that God can recognize must be established to start a new historical course. Jesus Christ came to this earth to establish the true standard of sons and daughters connected to the true standard of adopted children. To become a true child, one must establish the standard of adopted children and connect to it, and to become an adopted child, one must establish the standard of servants and connect to it. The witnesses of the era of Jesus, Anna and Simeon, all testified and appeared based on the standard of servants. By celebrating these days, the world can enter a new realm of fortune. When Jesus was about to die, there were the thieves on his right and left. The thief on the right is in the position that God exists, while the thief on the left is in the position that God does not exist. So what position does Barabbas hold? Barabbas represents the position of the Islamic authority. 

Let us become comrades in the establishment of the Unificationist world. Now we must understand that the time is coming when Jesus, who was crucified, will resurrect. 21) The Unification Church is the Indemnity Church
Today, it seems that the members of the Third Church have gathered the most. In any case, the Third Church is enthusiastic. The Teacher commends the members of the Third Church who gathered today, even those who contacted us this morning after knowing. The First Church is like the roots of a tree, the Second Church is like the trunk, and the Third Church is like the branches or leaves. Therefore, I thought the members of the Third Church would be excited, and sure enough, they are. People do not like to see the roots or trunk of a tree; they like to see the leaves. Thus, we have divided the Seoul church into three. The purpose of church activity is that religious people go forth centered on the spirit world. The person who prioritizes the perfection of spiritual personality is a religious person, and there are many such spiritualists in the Second Church compared to the First Church. Those who are here for the first time may not know what a spiritualist is. A spiritualist is someone who communicates with the spirit world and moves according to the instructions given from there. There are many such people in the Second Church. However, it is problematic if the Third Church continues to spread alone. It must spread but remain rooted in the First Church. 

285 The Unification Church is the Indemnity Church. You must become a branch belonging to the trunk and a leaf belonging to the branch. If the roots and trunk remain still while only the leaves flutter, what will happen? Can they come out? They cannot. Therefore, the members of the Third Church must know how great the grace of the First and Second Churches is and be grateful. (Laughter) Why are you laughing? That is the principle. Can you take the leaves of someone else's tree and attach them to your own tree and have them become the leaves of your own tree? Even if you graft thousands of leaves in a day, if they do not receive nutrients from the roots, no matter how much you try to graft, it will be useless. The Teacher quietly observes that the First and Second Churches seem to be moving toward the Third Church's way. Numerically, is the order going from Third to Second to First? That seems to be the Third Church's way of thinking. When counting, we count 1, 2, 3… so the members of the Third Church should have that kind of concept. However, the Teacher does not dislike gathering and working together. The Teacher also has that temperament. It is just that we must emphasize the overall connection. We are moving forward centered on this will to move the Republic of Korea and the world. Thus, heaven must come down, and we must rise. However, the stronger the descent, the more we can rise swiftly. You must value the historical connections we have built up until now. If you are in the Third Church, you must be fully loyal to the Third Church. However, there is something you must keep in mind. For example, no matter how much a person rises to become a leader who moves the world and governs the nation, there is something they must never forget: their hometown and the connection with their parents. Similarly, you must value the connections you have made. If you forget those, you will not be able to become a leader of that nation. Once, I heard that members of the Third Church only greet each other when they meet and do not ask more, just passing by. In the past, they would follow along to share their circumstances, and if someone spoke to them, they would be grateful, but that sentiment has disappeared, and only a lonely wind blows. Why is that? Perhaps it is because they fear that if they know the development of their church, the pastor will be stimulated and move vigorously, so they just greet and pass by. The Teacher knows everything you have done even if you remain quiet. Also, I know it even if you do not report it. 

The points to note in church activities: The Teacher supports the Third Church from the heart. Moreover, the Third Church is in the stages of revival, growth, and completion, which is wonderful. However, people forgive once and then again, but it is only at that moment. Their hearts turn away. Then what are they trying to do? Just wait and see what happens to such people. The teacher has walked this path, even if those whose hearts have turned that way have decided to “let’s endure.” What the teacher is most worried about now is about you. I want to take away everything I have given you until now and replace it. In the past, when local members came to see the teacher, he would run out to meet them even if he was sleeping. For whom did you come here? Did you come to be a plus for the teacher, or did you come to be a plus for God? Or did you come to be a plus for yourself? When commanded to do something, you do it, and when you see the tearful pleas, it seems like there are a few years left, but later it turns out that it is not so. God is the same. What the teacher is most afraid of is whether God will love as much as he promotes Korean people. If God does not love, I will also be moved. When it is said that I will be moved, it means that it is right to hold on. That time will surely come. When the teacher started this path, he left with nothing for his family to eat, carrying only a bag. When He says go, there are no excuses. He did not send a single letter or postcard home. He left thinking that if he didn’t die, he would meet again. We must go to find the heavenly path from a position of having cleared everything and being empty. Only then will God acknowledge it. If that happens, absolutely, one’s family will not starve to death. They may suffer for a few years, but once that time passes, their path will open, and my path will also become comfortable. Thus, the path of indemnity and restoration is harsh. When this happens, we can feel the heart of God when He lost Adam and Eve, and we can understand the heart of God looking at His children who left home.  
328 Let’s Fulfill Our Responsibilities. We all learn from that perspective. The teacher plans to tour the nation this week. Wherever he goes, he will have people check if there is a Unification Church there. If he is curious about a place, he will ask the children, “Is there a Unification Church here?” If there is no Unification Church, the teacher will not be able to hold his head up. At that time, he will have to pray before the Father for hours. It is time to restore families, and now you must know what time this is. Of course, the whole is important, but you must place your entire family, centered on your father and mother, before the will. So, just like when the teacher started the Unification Church, when friends come to your house, you should create a home where they can say, “Wow, this place is better than my house. Even if I eat barley rice or porridge, it is tastier than my home food. Just let me stay one more night.” A family that makes friends want to leave their own homes and come to yours will become a heavenly family. If there is anyone among the Unification Church members who has not thought about wanting to visit the headquarters where the teacher is, that person is not a Unification Church member. It is not because the teacher is lacking, but because the Unification Church members are lacking. Such a person is not a Unification Church member. The teacher is confident. There are no conditions before the will. It is unconditional. Since you have received without conditions, you must give without conditions. Because your mother and father gave birth to you, you must give unconditionally. That is how families must be restored. What you must take responsibility for is to repel the enemy Satan and liberate your parents and families. When that happens, national liberation will be achieved from there. Moreover, because parents love their children, it is easier to evangelize. It is rare for older people to even talk to their parents. However, you can evangelize your loving parents as much as you want. Knowing that this is the time, you must put your whole heart into evangelizing your parents. When you unite in one will and receive the blessings of heaven, creating a blessed family, there is no greater happiness than that. Know that this is a greater blessing than having hundreds of doctoral degrees, and I ask that you become those who fulfill the tremendous responsibility of restoration placed before you.  
23) Suffer in a Low Position  
<Summary of the Message> There is no true joy in a position that is being invaded. There is still struggle there. Therefore, we must stand on the ground where we have shed tears and blood from the very bottom. When the economy improves, we must help the family members who have suffered. The purpose of the fourfold movement is first to promote externally, second to allow the members to feel the new fortune of the providential time and undergo internal regeneration, third to create expectations for evangelizing established churches, and fourth to create opportunities to mobilize members. What God cannot be pleased with is that He is still standing in a position invaded by Satan. To love children, one must love them with a heart for the world. What has been devoted is not a failure, even if it fails. It contains the internal elements that can rise again. The teacher rebukes in front of the great ones so that their mistakes can be completely cleared. Also, the listeners sympathize. Because it happens in a place where the spirit world is watching, if they sympathize from the spirit world, it will be cleared up quickly. A filial child is someone who is often beaten with a heart centered on emotions. Abel is the one who is most often beaten centered on God’s will. Abel has conditions under which he can be beaten. If you strike Abel, someday Abel will have conditions to strike back at those who struck him several times. The Unification Church has developed because it has been well beaten from Abel’s position. Before the seven-year course ends, one should not hope to live well. One must go down to a low position to the point of feeling sorry for breathing, to the point of being ashamed to look at the sun and moon. God’s promise is the highest. To receive it, one must work hard. Do not hold onto resentment for long. If you hold onto resentment, even if someone prays for you, that prayer will rebound. The reason why amazing things do not happen in the spirit world in the local areas is the responsibility of the district leaders. What I fear the most is the lowering of the standard of the heart. When I was tortured by the Communists, my desire for revenge reached the heavens, but I could not strike before heaven struck, so I prayed for five or six hours. When I say, “Father!” when that heart is far away, I must desperately restore that heart. I must abandon a faith that is only a means. If I cannot stand on the highest standard of heart, I must at least stand in a position to receive sympathy from the members. Being high does not mean being high, and being low does not mean being low. If one establishes loyalty in a low place, they are alive. Now, I do not want to be in a position that makes God work hard. Therefore, let us not become those who owe debts through our devotion. The seven-year course... the time that comes only once is passing by. What will you leave behind at this time?  
24) God’s Heart and Our Responsibility  
Mark 15:34 <Summary of the Message> The land we live in cannot be called a world planned by God. No matter what you look at, it cannot be seen as a world where God’s will is fulfilled. Countless histories of sorrow have unfolded for the world to become this way. Whether it is personal sorrow, family sorrow, or any sorrow, it must be understood that it is not sorrow created among humans but sorrow caused by the battle between God and Satan. God, who wields the whip against His children to seek something greater, has been more sorrowful and miserable because the miserable affairs of humanity have been reflected in God’s heart. God has been more miserable than any individual, any nation, any country, or any world. No matter how miserable a person may be, there is no one more miserable than God. God has looked upon humanity with a heart more painful than a mother watching her beloved child die. To clear away this miserable and evil world today and to establish a world of goodness...
333 It is God's situation that things cannot be done. Humanity, born as fallen descendants, must establish conditions for restoration and seek the path of return. Our ancestors have suffered from those who opposed and persecuted them every time a new truth emerged. Throughout history, those sent by God have been given the mission to restore fallen humanity back to its original world, which meant that God had to push them into even more miserable circumstances than those of the fallen. You must understand this fact. God struck individuals to save families. In order to save something greater, He did not strike those who opposed but instead struck the sons and daughters who were raised in their place. You must remember that God's heart was indescribably pained when He wielded the whip against His children to save something greater. The path that the Israelite nation, which must be loyal to God, has taken has been accompanied by unspeakable suffering, and they have faced challenges on behalf of other nations. For this reason, God promised to send the Messiah to that miserable nation. Jesus was the hope of all history and the universe, a being that could not be exchanged for 4,000 years of history or anything else. Yet, Jesus was born in a miserable place, in a stable, and stood in a position where He could not reveal His identity and had to flee. Moreover, the high priests and scribes, who should have been loyal to Jesus, were not. Ultimately, the Israelite nation drove Jesus, who represented the purpose of human history and God's creation, to the path of the cross. God understood Jesus' situation better than anyone, but He could not overlook the personal circumstances outside of the principle. Thus, God could not directly protect Jesus until just before His death and had to stand in a position of abandonment. When Jesus cried out on the cross, “My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?” (Matthew 27:46), and God seemed indifferent, if Jesus had only intended to betray God, He could have completely turned against God's heart and our responsibility. You must understand that God, who could not face this miserable situation with acknowledgment, was even more miserable than Jesus. If there had been even a response of “Oh, my son!” when He cried out, “My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?” Jesus could have joyfully faced death. The loyalty of Jesus, who offered everything regardless of whether God accepted it or not, brought a new turning point in history. Such loyalty from Jesus could have turned the world of Satan around. Because God is the subject of love, He did not abandon even the fallen descendants but continued to look after them. God wanted to open a way for the forgiveness of humanity, which was being ravaged in the hands of Satan, even if it meant sacrificing Jesus. Therefore, God sought to save fallen humanity even at the cost of abandoning Jesus. Because of this, Jesus' death could indemnify the sacrifices of 4,000 years of history. The resurrection of Jesus meant that humanity could also resurrect thereafter. Now, after 2,000 years of history, the world is uniting around Christianity. God has judged. However, we must first understand whether to strike the enemy or to strike the beloved child first. Before the world is judged, there must be families, tribes, and nations that can represent the world. Judgment means striking the enemy. However, in order to execute judgment, there must first be a group that can stand in the position of representing heaven before striking down the world of the enemy. This group and this nation must inevitably weave a miserable history due to their historical connections. Today's Unification Church did not appear to judge the world but rather to stand in the position of receiving judgment before the world is judged. Therefore, we have been beaten personally, driven out of our families, and have suffered unjustly from our relatives. However, the more we find ourselves in such positions, the more we must dig deep into the ground and firmly establish our roots. Yet, many have grown weary in such positions. Many have hesitated, thinking the path ahead is long and arduous. However, you must know that the Father has not grown weary. We have sworn loyalty before God, and God has loved us. Therefore, we must become people who can say that even if heaven and earth change, we cannot sever our connection with God. Even in the situation of collapsing on Golgotha, crying out, “Abba Father, why have you forsaken me?” our heart must be greater in holding onto God than anything else. Through the loyal group that risks death, the new victory of resurrection will be achieved. We, the Unification group, must analyze ourselves once again from this perspective. We should find ourselves in the place of death, yet those who wish to avoid that place must be judged. What kind of position do you wish to go to in order to become a greater ship? Of course, you would want the highest position. And what kind of loyal child or faithful servant do you wish to be? A loyal child or faithful servant in a position that anyone can take is not significant. Jesus fulfilled loyalty and filial piety in a position that no one else could, which is why God could resurrect Him. However, Jesus was resurrected only as an individual. Therefore, we must resurrect Jesus in our families, in our nations, and in our world in the future. Only then can the history of resurrection unfold beyond the summit of Golgotha. 
336 When comparing the loyalty of the prophets and sages who have come and gone in history with our efforts, our efforts are so minimal that they are like floating clouds. Thus, our efforts are small. Nevertheless, the environment that has unfolded before us is enormous. Therefore, if there is effort, it must be acknowledged that God's effort is the greatest, and feeling ashamed and struggling in that light is the only normal attitude of faith. Let us remember the enormous fact that due to our mistakes, the processes of national and global judgment remain. The Unification Church that the teacher envisions and the Unification Church that you envision are vastly different. When viewed from the perspective of being the children of God's hope who have historically emerged, you stand at a very distant point. Of course, it is necessary to take pride in the past. However, today we must live looking toward the future. How can there be no path of Golgotha in the course of our lives? Only when the typhoon blows do we realize that even a large ship is small. We must have the determination to become a greater ship. The heart of the teacher regarding the will is impatient. This is not just my heart, but it is God's heart. Among 3 billion people, 30 million are falling into hell every year. Who can resist this death? Let us consider how urgent God's heart must be as He watches His dying children. Who can comfort the heart of such an urgent Father? Jesus could not do this either. That is why Jesus is returning to fulfill the unfulfilled desires of His heart. We are the warriors who have stepped onto the path of restoration. But where are we currently planting our flags? Have you ever felt that you cannot sleep peacefully in the coffin until the will of the great man is fulfilled? Is there not a warrior who is willing to jump into the enemy's territory with shells in order to save the nation and the world? Have you discovered yourself living in tears because you cannot fulfill your responsibilities, even though the path ahead is too long and overwhelming? Some members of the Unification Church sometimes feel that they are too shameless. I do not feel that way. The most serious concern I have as a leader is how to indemnify the path of the cross. If you understood that God is governing this nation through your struggles, there should be groups willing to struggle and serve. Nevertheless, many people run away at the slightest difficulty. No historical leader has started from a joyful position. Everyone has started from the worst, saddest positions. Jesus was oppressed from birth and sometimes had to eat the heads of grain because there was no food. However, because He could fulfill the principle of salvation, salvation was revealed through Him. The teacher does not wish to see glory in this generation. There are still contents around us that can cry out, “Abba Father! Why have you forsaken me? Why have you forsaken my family, my tribe, my nation?” If there is someone who truly knows this situation and can cry out like that, he can become the protagonist of the nation. The path to the cross does not lead to resurrection. It is only after crossing the cross that resurrection exists, a fact that no one has yet understood. No matter how beautiful the world may come, without concrete standards, it has nothing to do with me. Now, history is unfolding centered on the principle, so we must achieve the purpose of our faith. Regardless of our appearance, we must have the confidence that we are the sons and daughters recognized by God through blood and flesh. We must establish a connection with God through the seven-year course. To do this, we must stand in a position where we can receive God's compassion and love. In the remaining time, we earnestly hope to become one heart and one body and run together. 
338 Let us fulfill our responsibilities to achieve the will. The place where God can draw near is not the ordinary daily life environment you currently live in. Only after breaking through difficult adversities will God's grace be with you. You must establish a new connection with God beyond adversity for Him to be with you. What kind of heart should you have for the will to be fulfilled? Unification Church members cannot achieve the ideal world that God desires without leveling the high and low places surrounding them. Until now, there has not been a single son of true hope who can please God and make the universe rejoice. The reason heaven has been empty until today is that there has not been a true child of God's hope on earth. That heaven is undoubtedly a place where everyone wants to stay. However, since there have been no beloved children on this earth since the moment the ancestors of humanity fell, heaven has remained empty. For this reason, the entire universe has become an object of God's sorrow and has not been able to return joy to God. October 14, 1966 (Friday), noon, Gwangneung (located in Jinjup-myeon, Namyangju, Gyeonggi-do). * This message was given when the members of the Seoul First, Second, and Third Churches gathered in Gwangneung to commemorate the 16th anniversary of the teacher's release from Heungnam Prison, and it has been compiled from the December 1966 issue of <Seonghwa>, No. 61. The title was added by the editor.
340 Let us fulfill our responsibilities to achieve the will. You cannot serve both the world and God at the same time. That is why God has been carrying out the work of dividing this world until today. We, the Unification Church members, hope that the will will be fulfilled soon. Of course, the will must be fulfilled quickly. However, while hoping for the will to be fulfilled, there is no one taking responsibility to achieve it. If the will is to be fulfilled quickly, we cannot remain idle. We must not forget that God is continuously employing extraordinary strategies to achieve effective victory. God has been fighting for 6,000 years to effectively fulfill the will, and He is still fighting at this moment. However, the will is not fulfilled by God alone. There must be someone to fulfill the will. Until now, the history of sorrow has continued for 6,000 years because there has been no one who could fulfill the will. We are now saying that the ideology of the Unification Church is a heavenly ideology. However, in order to realize this ideology, is there anyone who has any achievements in relation to the God who has been earnest? Of course, the will must be fulfilled. However, for that will to be fulfilled, there must be corresponding achievements on my part. Without that, the heart that desires the will to be fulfilled may rather become a rebel against God, and you must understand this. Therefore, we must have something that can be a catalyst before all people. Why must the will be fulfilled? Those who think that fulfilling the will will make them better are rebels against God. Those who think that they will be materially happier than Americans, etc., are also rebels against heaven. We must hope for the will to be fulfilled from the perspective that when the will is fulfilled, God the Father will rest. On the day the will is fulfilled, I must prepare my wedding clothes and think that I will participate in this way. Without being able to present myself in a way that can appear before that Father who has historical grievances, I cannot appear before Him. 
341 You must think more and more about whether you have fulfilled your responsibilities with the heart that says, “I am rather afraid that the will will be fulfilled quickly. I am afraid that I may not have done what I should as a leader.” If you do not have the conditions to welcome the Father before the Father who has endured and waited, you will end up sending back the Father who has come to you after great hardships. We must be afraid that we might become those who rejoice at seeing our will spread everywhere and say, “Heaven, come quickly,” only to send God back again. Are you hoping for the will to be fulfilled quickly because you want to escape from the miserable environment you are in? Or are you hoping for the will to be fulfilled quickly to relieve the miserable cross that the Father is bearing? Analyzing that heart reveals whether you are on the side of Satan or God. Are you truly in a position to welcome the Father and let Him rest? Those who only pray, “God, please fulfill this,” are rebels who do not understand the heavenly mission. The Father must be welcomed on level ground, but since the Father is still on the battlefield, we must also defend that position. The more earnest the heart is for the will to be fulfilled, the more urgent the work becomes, and you must understand this. You must unify yourself to unify the world. You are living in anxiety and impatience, not knowing when you might change. Therefore, even in terms of heart, you do not know when you might betray God. Do you think that the environment we live in is an environment where God can be welcomed? Before the will is fulfilled, we must become members who fulfill the responsibilities to achieve the will. Can I truly claim to be living while holding onto the point of complete victory and peace? I must think about whether I can truly welcome the Father in the place where I live. We must quickly prepare the foundation for victory. God desires a level ground.
342   We must fulfill our responsibilities to achieve the purpose. That plain is a place that can only be reached after crossing the rugged mountains. Therefore, the path we walk must align with the path of atonement that God has walked. We are a group meant for unification, yet there are many among us who are not unified. Are you unified, everyone? First, I must be unified within myself. With a self that is not unified, I cannot unify anything. To unify, we must bind together our divided hearts. We must be willing to walk the path of death if called to do so. God is seeking a unified group. However, such a group has not been found. Throughout 4,000 years of history, there has only been one person, Jesus. God has been working throughout history so that everyone can take Jesus as a model to emulate. But since there has been no unification centered around Jesus, He must come again. The emergence of the Unification Church today is something that can bring great joy to God. For unification, we must pursue God even in the most difficult circumstances, centered on His historical heart. We must cross the Taesan mountains and reach the plain again so that Satan cannot accuse us. This place is a cosmic location for unification. Yet, people think that simply entering this place means they will all be unified here. For unification, a unified heart and ideology must be established, and through overcoming the path of suffering, the connection of hearts must arise from the marrow. Centering on Cheongpa-dong is merely a passing place. We must die under the ideology of unification, even if it means death. Unification is not done with the teacher but must first be achieved with God. Jacob unified God at the family level, Moses at the national level, and Jesus at the world level. Unifying with God cannot be achieved with just national standards. We must share a heart connection with heaven and earth. Regardless of personal difficulties, family hardships, or any challenges, if one works for God's will and falls, God cannot help but place them in a position of universal significance.  
343 When we say the purpose will be fulfilled, it is an incomprehensible heart to simply rejoice without understanding. We must think that the day when the purpose is fulfilled is a fearful day that should come quickly. A maiden of marriageable age must prepare and wait for the right time. Otherwise, the passing of age becomes a disaster. Become a group of unification that does not change until the end. Today is the day the teacher came out of prison. At that time, when the teacher was entering prison, he thought, "This is a label that God loves me." People like Yu Gwan-sun and Ahn Jung-geun have labels that the nation can love. To revive the spirit of the nation, we must elevate them. Even if driven to a place of death where one is opposed and persecuted, God longs for a son of loyalty and filial piety who can call Him Father. To comfort the Father even in a place of death is the greatest act of filial piety and loyalty, which is why for Jesus, the three hours just before His death became a greater stimulus for God's love than His 33 years of life. When the teacher entered prison with shackles, he took careful steps. When I am in a place of death or in prison, I thought about who could appear and become God's staff. Many were sent by God for me, but few remain, so they can only regret now. However, the teacher remains. When that person cannot fulfill their responsibility, God raises someone even greater. I am not lonely. The reason I have sent my family to the provinces to suffer is to make this era remembered by God and to quickly equip them with qualifications that heaven and earth can acknowledge. The teacher has little interest in those who have returned exhausted from the seven-year course. When I came here and saw the leaves falling from the trees in the wind, I felt, "There must be spring, summer, and autumn seasons in the Unification Church as well. Now, the winter season is coming."  
344   Let us fulfill our responsibilities to achieve the purpose. Every time the teacher sees you, he wants to scold and curse, but that is because it is autumn now. Soon it will be winter. When the harsh winter comes, where only the sound of cold wind can be heard, leaves that do not possess complete vitality will fall. What will the misery be like when those leaves fall? What kind of tree will remain in the end? Regardless of the changing seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter, the group of unification must embody the form of an evergreen tree that does not change. In spring, any tree can boast of its appearance, but few trees can survive through summer, autumn, and into winter. The group of unification must have a form that can remain green throughout the seasons. Therefore, even when a typhoon blows, we must not lose that appearance. When grafting, do not attach it to the branches but to the trunk. It is now dawn. Yet, everyone appears to be dozing off. Let us learn from the parable of the ten virgins of Jesus. The sight of blessed families falling exhausted is unbearable. How can one become a child of God if they cannot endure the seven years of the seven-year course? We are not a group that is unified. We are a group that unifies. We must not become flour; we must become yeast. Unification does not happen on the plain but must come out through the valley to the plain. Jesus also triumphed in the valley of death. This unification must be achieved through such victory. The teacher's wealth: The teacher has walked this path for 20 years but has not grown weary. The reason is that the father you call and the father I call have different emotional connections. It is because of the bond formed with the Father who has walked the path of hardship, even to prison, in a place of resentment and grievance. When the teacher was in prison, an enemy once came to visit to apologize.  
345 Whether to meet or not was a test. From God's perspective, there are people He might wish to eliminate and those who could become family. What must God's heart have been like to see such a situation? When the betrayers came to visit, I thought of God. God does not wish to have enemies, so I welcomed them with that heart. I then realized that the duty of filial piety I must perform before the Father who comes to me must also be done before my enemies. I knew that when I was with the Father, He always wanted to turn me around, even in the most painful circumstances. The God who sought me in the past is still with me when I pray for important matters. This is the wealth of the Unification Church. We must not avoid the environment but must digest it. The teacher received the exemplary worker award every year in Hungnam prison. There is no separate seed for workers. How can one fulfill heaven's will if they cannot become an active person who can digest the environment? Before going to work, I endured the biting cold of the body inspection for two hours. It is unimaginable how free it is to go out and work. Those who do not know this do not realize how good and precious a place prison is. God placed me in prison to train me for the purpose of establishing me in a position that no one can break. Because there is a standard of hardship in the past, even if there is hardship in the present life, I can endure it by thinking of that time. In a place like prison, a needle may not be worth much, but it is truly precious. I remember grinding a piece of glass to make a needle when I obtained a wire. Even now, if there are no side dishes, I think of the time when I ate plain rice. Back then, even cold water tasted good. That is why I still like cold water. The material scarcity was great, to the extent that I obtained a needle after three years, but in prison,  
346   Let us fulfill our responsibilities to achieve the purpose. The greatest hardship was hunger. Anyone who has fasted knows that in the cell, one can guess what food the neighbors are cooking. Just smelling that aroma could give one the strength to walk ten miles. I think of how God trained me and want to train you. What must the heart of a parent be like when their children ask for something they cannot give in a difficult situation? The teacher has walked the path of hardship, so any task is good. Hardship without value is useless, but the experience of hardship undertaken with a great purpose is invaluable, worth more than thousands of pieces of gold. This is the teacher's wealth. We are the mission bearers who must fulfill the purpose. The teacher has never prepared for a sermon. When speaking from mountain experiences, it is impossible not to be moved. When I think about why I endured hardship for the purpose in the past, it is because I lost my subjectivity. If I suffered for the nation, as long as the nation remains, the standard of that suffering also survives. However, if it is not for God, not for the nation, but for my own sake, when I grow weary, there is no way to recover. This is because there is nothing to stimulate me anew, even if I look around. No matter how much it is called the path of death, the altar of unification must be bound together and offered as a sacrifice. It must be a unification not for anyone but for God, for the nation and the people. Although you are people who must unify, you wish to be unified, and you are not even unified within yourselves. First, you must be unified and then move toward the position where you can unify others. You must not be dragged by God; you must take God with you.  
347 The place found after crossing the mountain and river is the true plain. Let us swear as we greet today. We are mission bearers who must fulfill the purpose and warriors in a position to unify. We must revive the established church for the second time. Now we must open the door to the established church anew. Otherwise, those people will become the most pitiful. We must evangelize Christians from the position of Joseph, who forgave his ten brothers who sold him into death, and open their doors. We must also open the doors of universities centered on the Principle Study Group. To open these two paths, we will not spare any money. We must not be stingy either. *
